   (añjalipadārthanirṇayaḥ) atrāpi devatābhayaprārthanādau dvayoḥ	(aQjali padArTa nirNayaH) atra api devatA Baya prArTana AdO dvayoH
   karayoratyantāṅgulisaṃśleṣaṇe 'ñjaliśabdārthatvasya dṛṣṭatvādañjalinā	karayoH atyanta aFguli saMSlezaNe aQjali Sabda arTa tvasya dRzwa tvAt aQjalinA
   pibedityādau jalagrahaṇasamarthavyākośātmakatvena	pibet iti AdO jala grahaNa samarTa vyAkoSa Atmaka tvena
   tadarthadarśanāddhomavākye sandehe	tad arTa darSanAt homa vAkye sandehe
   saktuhomarūpoddeśyatākāñjalividhisāmarthyānnirṇayaḥ, anyathā	saktu homa rUpa uddeSya tAkA aQjali viDi sAmarTyAt nirNayaH, anyaTA
   saktugrahaṇānupapatterityarthaḥ /	saktu grahaNa anupapatteH iti arTaH /
   vyākośātmaka iti viśabdasya vikasitārthatvāt	vyAkoSa AtmakaH iti viSabdasya vikasita arTa tvAt
   āṅaśceṣadarthakatvādīṣadvikasitakośapadavācyamukulākāra ityarthaḥ //	AFaH ca Izat arTaka tvAt Izadvikasita koSa pada vAcya mukula AkAraH iti arTaH //
   (anyathānupapattisahakṛtasyaiva sāmarthyasya nirṇāyakatvāt	(anyaTA anupapatti saha kRtasya eva sAmarTyasya nirNAyaka tvAt 
   puroḍāśāvadānena svadhitiprāptiriti nirūpaṇam) atraca na kevalaṃ	puroxASa avadAnena svaDiti prAptiH iti nirUpaNam) atra ca na kevalam
   sāmarthyamātrādeva vyavasthā, tathātve svadhiterapi puroḍāśāvadāne	sAmarTya mAtrAt eva vyavasTA, taTA tve svaDiteH api puroxASa avadAne
   sāmarthyasattvena māṃsāvadānavyavasthāyā asiddheḥ,	sAmarTya sattvena mAMsa avadAna vyavasTAyAH asidDeH,
   kintvanyathānupapattisahitāt tasmāt /	kintu anyaTA anupapatti sahitAt tasmAt /

   svadhitiprayojakatvaṃ kalpanīyamityapi jñeyam //	svaDiti prayojaka tvam kalpanIyam iti api jQeyam //
   (vāśabdaghaṭitasyāpyadhikaraṇāntaratayā yojanam) yadyapi cārthādveti sūtre	(vA Sabda Gawitasya api aDikaraNa antara tayA yojanam) yadi api ca arTAt vA iti sUtre
   vāśabdopādānabalādaikādhikaraṇyameva pūrvasūtraikavākyatayā bhāti;	vA Sabda upAdAna balAt a eka ADikaraNyam eva pUrva sUtra eka vAkya tayA BAti;
   tathāpyekavākyopāttaikadeśaśabdasyārthadvayaparatvānupapatteranuṣaktasya	taTA api eka vAkya upAtta eka deSa Sabdasya arTa dvaya paratva anupapatteH anuzaktasya
   vākyāntarārthabhede bādhakābhāvamabhipretyādhikaraṇāntaraparatayā	vAkya antara arTa Bede bADaka aBAvam aBipretya aDikaraNa antara para tayA
   bhāṣyakārādivyākhyānaṃ draṣṭavyam /	BAzya kAra Adi vyAKyAnam drazwavyam /
   asmiṃśca vākye pradātavye ityapi padaṃ kaustubhe dhṛtaṃ	asmin= ca vAkye pradAtavye iti api padam kOstuBe DRtam
   tasyāhavanīyolmukena mahāvedyāstṛtabarhiṣonte dāhādutthito	tasya AhavanIya ulmukena mahA vedya AstRta barhizonte dAhAt utTitaH 
   vaiśvānarognirartho draṣṭavyaḥ /	vESvAnara ugniH arTaH drazwavyaH /

   smṛtyācārayostadapekṣayā prāthamyenopādānam /	smRti AcArayoH tad apekzayA prATamyena upAdAnam /
   mānādhīnatvena meyasiddherāvaśyakasya pramāṇanirūpaṇasyottaratra nirūpaṇe	mAna aDIna tvena meya sidDeH AvaSyakasya pramANa nirUpaNasya uttaratra nirUpaNe
   hetutvasūcanadvārā vakṣyamāṇādhyāyārthān śiṣyoparamanirāsārthaṃ	hetu tva sUcana dvArAH vakzyamANa aDyAya arTAn Sizya uparama nirAsa arTam
   pratijānīte           ataḥparamiti //	pratijAnIte          atas param iti //
